type is reachable, comparing functors and clusters, and a procedure to
skip loci in a predicate.

The lexemes can be compared with each other.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{123}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}}}\moddef{Compare lexeme pointers~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-2z38Iw-2}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{CompareLexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}(aKey1, aKey2: Pointer): Integer;
var
   lInt: integer;
begin
   lInt:=CompareInt(ord(\nwlinkedidentc{LexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4dPUWz-1}(aKey1)^.fLexem.Kind),ord(\nwlinkedidentc{LexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4dPUWz-1}(aKey2)^.fLexem.Kind));
   if lInt <> 0 then
   begin
      \nwlinkedidentc{CompareLexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}:=lInt;
      exit;
   end;
   lInt:=CompareInt(\nwlinkedidentc{LexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4dPUWz-1}(aKey1)^.fLexem.Nr,\nwlinkedidentc{LexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4dPUWz-1}(aKey2)^.fLexem.Nr);
   if lInt <> 0 then
   begin
      \nwlinkedidentc{CompareLexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}:=lInt;
      exit;
   end;
   \nwlinkedidentc{CompareLexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1} := 0;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CompareLexemPtr}}{CompareLexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3J7fci-1}\eatline

function \nwlinkedidentc{MSortedLexemList}{NW3BJgTc-1vNvbY-1}\nwlinkedidentc{.IndexOfLexem}{NW3BJgTc-1C1xuS-1}(const aLexem: Lexem): Integer;
var
   I: Integer;
   lLexemObj: \nwlinkedidentc{LexemObj}{NW3BJgTc-4dPUWz-1};
begin
   IndexOfLexem := -1;
   if @fCompare = nil then
   begin
      ListError(coSortedListError,0);
      exit;
   end;
   lLexemObj.Init(aLexem);
   if Find(@lLexemObj, I) then
   begin
      if I < Count then IndexOfLexem := fIndex^[I];
   end;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{MSortedLexemList.IndexOfLexem}}{MSortedLexemList.IndexOfLexem}{NW3BJgTc-1C1xuS-1}\eatline
\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-Pq1E3-1}}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{MSortedLexemList.IndexOfLexem}}{MSortedLexemList.IndexOfLexem}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{LexemObj}}{LexemObj}}\\{{\nwixident{MSortedLexemList}}{MSortedLexemList}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LexemObj}}{LexemObj}{NW3BJgTc-1C1xuS-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{MSortedLexemList}}{MSortedLexemList}{NW3BJgTc-1C1xuS-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{132}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{133}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-2lGhJZ-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2lGhJZ-1}}}\moddef{Get the object for a lexeme from a lexeme list~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2lGhJZ-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-Pq1E3-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{MSortedLexemList}{NW3BJgTc-1vNvbY-1}.ObjectOf(const aLexem: Lexem): \nwlinkedidentc{LexemPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4dPUWz-1};
var
   I: integer;
begin
   ObjectOf := nil;
   I := IndexOfLexem(aLexem);
   if I>=0 then ObjectOf := Items^[I];
end;

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{143}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-46EOn0-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-46EOn0-1}}}\moddef{Insert an object at a lexeme in a \code{}MLexemAndListList\edoc{}~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-46EOn0-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-1V2Qm1-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
procedure \nwlinkedidentc{MLexemAndListList}{NW3BJgTc-4RecXS-1}\nwlinkedidentc{.InsertAtlexem}{NW3BJgTc-46EOn0-1}( aLexem: Lexem; aItem: Pointer);
var
   lLexemPtr: \nwlinkedidentc{MLexemAndListPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4E8EdJ-1};
begin
   lLexemPtr := \nwlinkedidentc{MLexemAndListPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4E8EdJ-1}(ObjectOf(aLexem));
   if lLexemPtr = nil then
   begin
      lLexemPtr:=new(\nwlinkedidentc{MLexemAndListPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4E8EdJ-1},Init(aLexem));
      Insert(lLexemPtr);
   end;
   lLexemPtr^.fList.Insert(aItem);
end;

\subsection{Collecting Terms}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{145}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}}\moddef{Collecting terms implementation~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-KFHEF-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\LA{}Skip loci in a predicate~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Compare term lists~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Compare attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Compare type collections~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2RQuXV-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Compare types~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2zyXeU-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Compare formulas~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Size of a term list~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-qRRhl-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Size of type~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2QAVHq-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}Size of a term~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-1G2NjT-1}}\RA{}

\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-KFHEF-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{146}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{147}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}}}\moddef{Skip loci in a predicate~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
procedure \nwlinkedidentc{SkipLocPred}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}(var aFrm: \nwlinkedidentc{FrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1});
var
   lFrm: \nwlinkedidentc{FrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
begin
   repeat
      while aFrm^.FrmSort=ikFrmPrivPred do
         if \nwlinkedidentc{LocPredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2t9tGv-1}(aFrm)^.PredExp^.FrmSort = ikError then exit
         else aFrm:=\nwlinkedidentc{LocPredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2t9tGv-1}(aFrm)^.PredExp;
      if (aFrm^.FrmSort=ikFrmNeg)
         and (\nwlinkedidentc{NegFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2U2t6u-1}(aFrm)^.NegArg^.FrmSort = ikFrmPrivPred) then
      begin
         lFrm:=\nwlinkedidentc{LocPredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2t9tGv-1}(\nwlinkedidentc{NegFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2U2t6u-1}(aFrm)^.NegArg)^.PredExp;
         if lFrm^.FrmSort = ikError then exit;
         while lFrm^.FrmSort=ikFrmPrivPred do
            lFrm:=\nwlinkedidentc{LocPredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2t9tGv-1}(lFrm)^.PredExp;
         if lFrm^.FrmSort = ikError then exit;
         if lFrm^.FrmSort = ikFrmNeg then
            aFrm:=\nwlinkedidentc{NegFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2U2t6u-1}(lFrm)^.NegArg;
      end
   until aFrm^.FrmSort<>ikFrmPrivPred;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SkipLocPred}}{SkipLocPred}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}\eatline
\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SkipLocPred}}{SkipLocPred}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{FrmPtr}}{FrmPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{LocPredFrmPtr}}{LocPredFrmPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{NegFrmPtr}}{NegFrmPtr}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FrmPtr}}{FrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LocPredFrmPtr}}{LocPredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{NegFrmPtr}}{NegFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{148}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{149}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}}}\moddef{Compare term lists~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}(fTrm1,fTrm2:\nwlinkedidentc{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}):integer; forward;

function \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrmLists}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}(fTrmList1,fTrmList2: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmList}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): integer;
var
   lInt: integer;
   \{! uwaga zaklada sie ze lsity sa rowne !\}
   \{! note, it is assumed that the numbers are equal!\}
begin
   \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrmLists}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}:=0;
   while fTrmList1 <> nil do
   begin lInt:=\nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}(fTrmList1^.XTrmPtr,fTrmList2^.XTrmPtr);
      if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrmLists}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}:=lInt; exit end;
      fTrmList1:=fTrmList1^.NextTrm;
      fTrmList2:=fTrmList2^.NextTrm;
   end;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CompareTrmLists}}{CompareTrmLists}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}\eatline
\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CompareTrmLists}}{CompareTrmLists}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{CompareTrms}}{CompareTrms}}\\{{\nwixident{TrmList}}{TrmList}}\\{{\nwixident{TrmPtr}}{TrmPtr}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CompareTrms}}{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TrmList}}{TrmList}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TrmPtr}}{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{150}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{151}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}}}\moddef{Compare attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-3Ag9Op-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{CompareAttr}{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}(aAttr1, aAttr2: \nwlinkedidentc{AttrPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): Integer;
var
   lInt,lAttrNr1,lAttrNr2: integer;
   lArgs1,lArgs2: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmList}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
begin
   aAttr1^.AdjustAttr(lAttrNr1,lArgs1);
   aAttr2^.AdjustAttr(lAttrNr2,lArgs2);
   lInt:=CompareInt(lAttrNr1,lAttrNr2);
   if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareAttr}{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}:=lInt; exit end;
   lInt:=CompareInt(ord(aAttr1^.fNeg),ord(aAttr2^.fNeg));
   if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareAttr}{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}:=lInt; exit end;
   \nwlinkedidentc{CompareAttr}{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}:=\nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrmLists}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}(lArgs1,lArgs2);
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CompareAttr}}{CompareAttr}{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}\eatline

   i,lInt: integer;

   for i:=0 to aClu1^.Count-1 do
   begin
      lInt:=\nwlinkedidentc{CompareAttr}{NW3BJgTc-2FvPQE-1}(\nwlinkedidentc{AttrPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}(\nwlinkedidentc{AttrCollectionPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}(aClu1)^.Items^[i]),\nwlinkedidentc{AttrPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}(\nwlinkedidentc{AttrCollectionPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}(aClu2)^.Items^[i]));
      if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareClusters}{NW3BJgTc-qDRfb-1}:=lInt; exit end;
   end;
   \nwlinkedidentc{CompareClusters}{NW3BJgTc-qDRfb-1}:=0;
end;

   end;

function \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1}(fFrm1,fFrm2: \nwlinkedidentc{FrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): integer;
var
   lInt,k: integer;
begin
   \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := 0;
   \nwlinkedidentc{SkipLocPred}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}(fFrm1);
   // \nwlinkedidentc{SkipLocPred}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}(fFrm1); To be checked later whether \nwlinkedidentc{SkipLocPred}{NW3BJgTc-3AIWzL-1}(fFrm2) is not needed here!!!
   lInt := CompareInt(ord(fFrm1^.FrmSort),ord(fFrm2^.FrmSort));
   if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := lInt; exit end;
   case fFrm1^.FrmSort of
      ikFrmVerum,ikFrmThesis: ;
      ikFrmNeg: \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1}(\nwlinkedidentc{NegFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2U2t6u-1}(fFrm1)^.NegArg,\nwlinkedidentc{NegFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-2U2t6u-1}(fFrm2)^.NegArg);
      ikFrmQual:
         with \nwlinkedidentc{QualFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3qoO2q-1}(fFrm1)^ do
      begin
         lInt := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}(QualTrm,\nwlinkedidentc{QualFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3qoO2q-1}(fFrm2)^.QualTrm);
         if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := lInt; exit end;
         \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTyps}{NW3BJgTc-2zyXeU-1}(QualTyp,\nwlinkedidentc{QualFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3qoO2q-1}(fFrm2)^.QualTyp);
      end;
      ikFrmConj:
         with \nwlinkedidentc{ConjFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-CUFeP-1}(fFrm1)^ do
      begin
         lInt := CompareInt(Conjuncts.Count,\nwlinkedidentc{ConjFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-CUFeP-1}(fFrm2)^.Conjuncts.Count);
         if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := lInt; exit end;
         for k := 0 to Conjuncts.Count-1 do
         begin
            lInt := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1}(Conjuncts.Items^[k],\nwlinkedidentc{ConjFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-CUFeP-1}(fFrm2)^.Conjuncts.Items^[k]);
            if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := lInt; exit end;
         end;
      end;
      ikFrmSchPred,ikFrmAttr,ikFrmPrivPred,ikFrmPred:
         with \nwlinkedidentc{PredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-PvUzk-1}(fFrm1)^ do
      begin
         lInt := CompareInt(PredNr,\nwlinkedidentc{PredFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-PvUzk-1}(fFrm2)^.PredNr);
         if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := lInt; exit end;

      end;
      ikFrmUniv:
         with \nwlinkedidentc{UnivFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4c2u0P-1}(fFrm1)^ do
      begin
         lInt := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTyps}{NW3BJgTc-2zyXeU-1}(Quantified,\nwlinkedidentc{UnivFrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4c2u0P-1}(fFrm2)^.Quantified);
         if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1} := lInt; exit end;

      end;
      ikError: ;
   else RunTimeError(2049);
   end;
end;

function \nwlinkedidentc{SizeOfTrmList}{NW3BJgTc-qRRhl-1}(fTrmList: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmList}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): integer;
var
   s: integer;
begin
   s := 0;
   while fTrmList <> nil do
      with fTrmList^ do
   begin
      inc(s,\nwlinkedidentc{SizeOfTrm}{NW3BJgTc-1G2NjT-1}(XTrmPtr));
      fTrmList := NextTrm;
   end;
   \nwlinkedidentc{SizeOfTrmList}{NW3BJgTc-qRRhl-1} := s;
end;

function \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}(fTrm1,fTrm2: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): integer;
var
   lInt: integer;
begin
   \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := 0;
   lInt := CompareInt(\nwlinkedidentc{SizeOfTrm}{NW3BJgTc-1G2NjT-1}(fTrm1),\nwlinkedidentc{SizeOfTrm}{NW3BJgTc-1G2NjT-1}(fTrm2));
   if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := lInt; exit end;
   while fTrm1^.TrmSort=ikTrmPrivFunc do
      if \nwlinkedidentc{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-9mI19-1}(fTrm1)^.FuncExp^.TrmSort=ikError then break
      else fTrm1 := \nwlinkedidentc{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-9mI19-1}(fTrm1)^.FuncExp;
   while fTrm2^.TrmSort=ikTrmPrivFunc do
      if \nwlinkedidentc{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-9mI19-1}(fTrm2)^.FuncExp^.TrmSort=ikError then break
      else fTrm2 := \nwlinkedidentc{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-9mI19-1}(fTrm2)^.FuncExp;
   with fTrm1^ do
   begin
      lInt := CompareInt(ord(TrmSort),ord(fTrm2^.TrmSort));
      if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := lInt; exit end;
      case TrmSort of
         ikTrmLocus,ikTrmBound,ikTrmConstant,ikTrmInfConst,ikTrmFreeVar,ikTrmLambdaVar,ikTrmNumeral,ikTrmEqConst:
            with \nwlinkedidentc{VarTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-1BIExP-1}(fTrm1)^ do
         begin
            \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := CompareInt(VarNr,\nwlinkedidentc{VarTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-1BIExP-1}(fTrm2)^.VarNr);
         end;
         ikTrmSchFunc,ikTrmAggreg,ikTrmPrivFunc,ikTrmFunctor,ikTrmSelector:
            with \nwlinkedidentc{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-40ndBy-1}(fTrm1)^ do
         begin
            lInt := CompareInt(FuncNr,\nwlinkedidentc{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-40ndBy-1}(fTrm2)^.FuncNr);
            if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := lInt; exit end;
            \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrmLists}{NW3BJgTc-35PipB-1}(FuncArgs,\nwlinkedidentc{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-40ndBy-1}(fTrm2)^.FuncArgs);
         end;
         ikTrmFraenkel:
            with \nwlinkedidentc{FraenkelTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-1WrvsE-1}(fTrm1)^  do
         begin
            lInt := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}(LambdaScope,\nwlinkedidentc{FraenkelTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-1WrvsE-1}(fTrm2)^.LambdaScope);
            if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := lInt; exit end;
            lInt := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareFrms}{NW3BJgTc-45tnz9-1}(Compr,\nwlinkedidentc{FraenkelTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-1WrvsE-1}(fTrm2)^.Compr);
            if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := lInt; exit end;
            \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTypColls}{NW3BJgTc-2RQuXV-1}(LambdaArgs,\nwlinkedidentc{FraenkelTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-1WrvsE-1}(fTrm2)^.LambdaArgs);
         end;
         ikTrmChoice:
            \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTyps}{NW3BJgTc-2zyXeU-1}(ChoiceTrmPtr(fTrm1)^.ChoiceTyp,
                                       ChoiceTrmPtr(fTrm2)^.ChoiceTyp);
         ikTrmQua:
            with \nwlinkedidentc{QuaTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-32FqXh-1}(fTrm1)^ do
         begin
            lInt := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}(TrmProper,\nwlinkedidentc{QuaTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-32FqXh-1}(fTrm2)^.TrmProper);
            if lInt <> 0 then begin \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := lInt; exit end;
            \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1} := \nwlinkedidentc{CompareTyps}{NW3BJgTc-2zyXeU-1}(Qua,\nwlinkedidentc{QuaTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-32FqXh-1}(fTrm2)^.Qua);
         end;
         ikTrmIt: ;
      else
      begin
         \{$IFDEF MDEBUG\}
         writeln(InfoFile,'CompareTrms:TrmSort=',TrmSort,'|');
         \{$ENDIF\}
         RunTimeError(2341);
      end;
      end;
   end;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CompareTrms}}{CompareTrms}{NW3BJgTc-37u0kw-1}\eatline

\subsection{Term-Type Collections}

We track the types of terms in a {\Tt{}\nwlinkedidentq{TTCollection}{NW3BJgTc-34g5el-1}\nwendquote}, which is an key-value
dictionary.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{181}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}}}\moddef{Round up type for a term with a given type~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-3JYDsp-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}(lTyp: \nwlinkedidentc{TypPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}; fTrm: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): \nwlinkedidentc{TypPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
var
   i,lLeft,lRight: integer;
   lClusterPtr: \nwlinkedidentc{AttrCollectionPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
   lFunctorCluster: \nwlinkedidentc{FClusterPtr}{NW3BJgTc-20ApBH-1};
   lKey: \nwlinkedidentc{FClusterObj}{NW3BJgTc-3I7ztq-1};
   lIntSet: IntSet;
label Inconsistent\{,1\};
begin
   if fTrm^.TrmSort in [ikTrmFunctor,ikTrmSelector,ikTrmAggreg] then
   begin
      lClusterPtr := CopyCluster(lTyp^.UpperCluster);
      lKey.nClusterTerm := fTrm;
      if \nwlinkedidentc{FunctorCluster}{NW3BJgTc-3iu0LI-7}.FindInterval( @lKey, lLeft, lRight) then
      begin
         i := lLeft;
         lIntSet.Init(0);
         while i <= lRight do
         begin
            if not lIntSet.IsInSet(i) then
            begin lFunctorCluster := \nwlinkedidentc{FunctorCluster}{NW3BJgTc-3iu0LI-7}.AtIndex(i);
            if RoundUpWith(lFunctorCluster,fTrm,lTyp,lClusterPtr) then
            begin
               lClusterPtr^.RoundUpWith(lTyp);
               dispose(lTyp^.UpperCluster,Done);
               lTyp^.UpperCluster := lClusterPtr;
               if not lClusterPtr^.fConsistent then
               begin
                  lIntSet.Done;
                  goto Inconsistent;
               end;
               lClusterPtr := CopyCluster(lTyp^.UpperCluster);
               lIntSet.Insert(i);
               if lFunctorCluster^.nClusterType <> nil then
               begin i := lLeft; continue end;
            end
            else if lFunctorCluster^.nClusterType = nil then
               lIntSet.Insert(i);
            end;
            inc(i);
         end;
         lIntSet.Done;
      end;
      Inconsistent:
   end;
   \nwlinkedidentc{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1} := lTyp;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}}{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\eatline
\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-3JYDsp-1}}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}}{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{AttrCollectionPtr}}{AttrCollectionPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{FClusterObj}}{FClusterObj}}\\{{\nwixident{FClusterPtr}}{FClusterPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{FunctorCluster}}{FunctorCluster}}\\{{\nwixident{TrmPtr}}{TrmPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{TypPtr}}{TypPtr}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{AttrCollectionPtr}}{AttrCollectionPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FClusterObj}}{FClusterObj}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FClusterPtr}}{FClusterPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FunctorCluster}}{FunctorCluster}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TrmPtr}}{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TypPtr}}{TypPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{182}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{183}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}}}\moddef{Insert a term into a TT collection~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-3JYDsp-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{InsertTermInTTColl}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}(fTrm: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): integer;
var
   lPlace,i: integer;
   lTTPairPtr: \nwlinkedidentc{TTPairPtr}{NW3BJgTc-34g5el-1};
   lClusterPtr: \nwlinkedidentc{AttrCollectionPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
   lTrmList: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmList}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
   lTrm: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1};
begin
   case fTrm^.TrmSort of
      ikTrmFunctor,ikTrmSelector,ikTrmAggreg:
         begin
            with \nwlinkedidentc{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-40ndBy-1}(fTrm)^ do
            begin
               lTrmList := FuncArgs;
               while lTrmList<>nil do
               begin
                  lTrm := lTrmList^.XTrmPtr;
                  while lTrm^.TrmSort=ikTrmPrivFunc do
                     if \nwlinkedidentc{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-9mI19-1}(lTrm)^.FuncExp^.TrmSort=ikError then break
                     else lTrm := \nwlinkedidentc{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-9mI19-1}(lTrm)^.FuncExp;
                  if lTrm^.TrmSort in [ikTrmFunctor,ikTrmSelector,ikTrmAggreg] then
                     \nwlinkedidentc{InsertTermInTTColl}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}(lTrm);
                  lTrmList := lTrmList^.NextTrm;
               end;
            end;
         end;
   end;
   with gTermCollection do
      if not Search(fTrm,lPlace) then
      begin
         lTTPairPtr := new(\nwlinkedidentc{TTPairPtr}{NW3BJgTc-34g5el-1},Init(fTrm));
         AtInsert(lPlace,lTTPairPtr);
         lTTPairPtr^.nTyp := \nwlinkedidentc{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}{NW3BJgTc-3HBCgY-1}(lTTPairPtr^.nTyp,fTrm);
         lClusterPtr := CopyCluster(lTTPairPtr^.nTyp^.UpperCluster);
         lClusterPtr^.RoundUpWith(lTTPairPtr^.nTyp);
         dispose(lTTPairPtr^.nTyp^.UpperCluster,Done);
         lTTPairPtr^.nTyp^.UpperCluster := lClusterPtr;
         for i  :=  0 to Count-1 do
            if lTTPairPtr = Items^[i] then
            begin
               lPlace := i;
               break
            end;
         //    Search(fTrm,lPlace);       // np. nie dziala w przypadku argumentow z fraenkelem
         \{ e.g. it does not work with fraenkel arguments \}
         mizassert(2888,lPlace>=0);
         // moga pojawic sie termy w  wyniku zawolania procedur RoundUp zmieni sie index termu na kolekcji posortowanej
         \{ terms may appear as a result of calling the RoundUp 
           procedures, the index of the term on the sorted collection 
           will change \} 
      end;
   result := lPlace;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{InsertTermInTTColl}}{InsertTermInTTColl}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\eatline
\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-3JYDsp-1}}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{InsertTermInTTColl}}{InsertTermInTTColl}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{AttrCollectionPtr}}{AttrCollectionPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{FuncTrmPtr}}{FuncTrmPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{LocFuncTrmPtr}}{LocFuncTrmPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}}{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}}\\{{\nwixident{TrmList}}{TrmList}}\\{{\nwixident{TrmPtr}}{TrmPtr}}\\{{\nwixident{TTPairPtr}}{TTPairPtr}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{AttrCollectionPtr}}{AttrCollectionPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FuncTrmPtr}}{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LocFuncTrmPtr}}{LocFuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}}{RoundUpTrmTypeWithType}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TrmList}}{TrmList}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TrmPtr}}{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TTPairPtr}}{TTPairPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3ksvI3-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{184}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{185}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-3AZVMl-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3AZVMl-1}}}\moddef{Remove terms from a TT Collection~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-3AZVMl-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{NW3BJgTc-3JYDsp-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
procedure \nwlinkedidentc{RemoveTermsFromTTColl}{NW3BJgTc-3AZVMl-1};
var
   k: integer;
begin
   dec(gTermScope);
   with gTermCollection do
      for k := 0 to Count-1 do
         if \nwlinkedidentc{TTPairPtr}{NW3BJgTc-34g5el-1}(Items^[k])^.nTermScope > gTermScope then
         begin
            dispose(\nwlinkedidentc{TTPairPtr}{NW3BJgTc-34g5el-1}(Items^[k]),Done);
            Items^[k] := nil
         end;
   gTermCollection.Pack;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RemoveTermsFromTTColl}}{RemoveTermsFromTTColl}{NW3BJgTc-3AZVMl-1}\eatline
\nwused{\\{NW3BJgTc-3JYDsp-1}}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RemoveTermsFromTTColl}}{RemoveTermsFromTTColl}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{TTPairPtr}}{TTPairPtr}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TTPairPtr}}{TTPairPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3AZVMl-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{186}\nwdocspar
\subsection{}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{187}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}}}\moddef{Functor redefinition~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
function \nwlinkedidentc{FuncRedefNr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}(fNr: integer): integer;
begin
   with \nwlinkedidentc{ConstrPtr}{NW3BJgTc-AAs3k-1}( \nwlinkedidentc{Constr}{NW3BJgTc-4ReYNr-1}[ coFunctor].Items^[ fNr])^ do
      if fWhichConstrNr <> 0 then
         \nwlinkedidentc{FuncRedefNr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1} :=  fWhichConstrNr
      else \nwlinkedidentc{FuncRedefNr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1} :=  fNr;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{FuncRedefNr}}{FuncRedefNr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}\eatline
\nwnotused{Functor redefinition}\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{FuncRedefNr}}{FuncRedefNr}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{Constr}}{Constr}}\\{{\nwixident{ConstrPtr}}{ConstrPtr}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{Constr}}{Constr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ConstrPtr}}{ConstrPtr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{188}\nwdocspar
A simple function which places {\Tt{}ikTrmFunctors\nwendquote} before all other
{\Tt{}ikTerm\nwendquote} instances.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{189}\sublabel{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1}}}\moddef{Compare functor terms~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
// this is now very simple, ikTrmFunctor > any other ikTrm,
// all other ikTrm equal, and two ikTrmFunctor by adjusted number
function \nwlinkedidentc{CmpFuncTrm}{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1}(fTrm1,fTrm2: \nwlinkedidentc{TrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-3eikUI-1}): integer;
begin
   if fTrm1^.TrmSort <> ikTrmFunctor then
   begin
      if fTrm2^.TrmSort <> ikTrmFunctor then \nwlinkedidentc{CmpFuncTrm}{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1} :=  0
      else \nwlinkedidentc{CmpFuncTrm}{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1} :=  -1
   end
   else
   begin
      if fTrm2^.TrmSort <> ikTrmFunctor then \nwlinkedidentc{CmpFuncTrm}{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1} :=  1
      else
         \nwlinkedidentc{CmpFuncTrm}{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1}  :=  CompareInt( \nwlinkedidentc{FuncRedefNr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}( \nwlinkedidentc{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-40ndBy-1}( fTrm1)^.FuncNr),
                                     \nwlinkedidentc{FuncRedefNr}{NW3BJgTc-4WzeTx-1}( \nwlinkedidentc{FuncTrmPtr}{NW3BJgTc-40ndBy-1}( fTrm2)^.FuncNr));
   end;
end;
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CmpFuncTrm}}{CmpFuncTrm}{NW3BJgTc-21rr69-1}\eatline
